Customer Profiles Upload Tool:

 

Steps in Uploading Customer Profiles:

 

  1. Prepare an input file, which is of “CSV” format (Comma Separated Format). This format can be = get –

·        Open an Ex= cel Spread sheet

·        Add all th= e data in the format mention in the instructions-

·        First Colu= mn – Oracle Customer Account Number  

·        Second Col= umn - Payment Term  

·        Third Colu= mn - Credit Checking Flag  

·        Fourth Col= umn - Dunning Letters Flag

·        Fifth Colu= mn - Dunning Letters Set

·        Sixth Colu= mn - Credit Hold Flag    

·        Seventh Co= lumn - Collector Name  

 

Note that if any of the above columns are null, please leave the value as null. = BUT, if you leave the last column also null, then Micro Soft Excel does not put = the commas as desired and the file format may be wrong and you may get errors in the file upload. After the data is added in Excel spread sheet, save it as “Comma Separated Values” format, as shown in = the screen shot.

 

<= ![endif]>

 

So, a typical input file, when opened in a notepad, looks like this-=

 

Orig_System_Reference,Collector_Name,payment_terms,credit_checking,dunning_= letters,dunning_letter_set,credit_hold

account_number,payment_terms,credit_checking,dunning_letters,dunning= _letter_set,credit_hold,Collector_Name

126769,NET 30,Y,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

1096,,,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

126846,,,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

 

In another example, say there are 3 records and record 2 and 3 do not have val= ues for  payment_terms and credit_checking. The file will look like the below in Excel-

 

account_number

payment_terms

credit_checking

dunning_letters

dunning_letter_set

credit_hold

Collector_Name

126769

N= ET 30

Y=

Y=

S= TANDARD_OD

&= nbsp;

11003

1096

&= nbsp;

&= nbsp;

Y=

S= TANDARD_OD

&= nbsp;

11003

126846

&= nbsp;

&= nbsp;

Y=

S= TANDARD_OD

&= nbsp;

11003

 

 

In notepad the above file will look like-

account_number,payment_terms,credit_checking,dunning_letters,dunning= _letter_set,credit_hold,Collector_Name

126769,NET 30,Y,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

1096,,,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

126846,,,Y,STANDARD_OD,,11003

 

  1. Select the file from the local using “Browse…” button in the page.

<= ![endif]>

  1. That’s it!!
  2. This file will be uploaded into server. A concurrent request set will be submitted in the background to synch the customer profiles into CDH registry (TCA registry). The tool shows a confirmation message telling that the file <fi= le_name> has been uploaded into the server; And a re= quest set, <request_number> has been submi= tted in the back ground. Please check the concurrent request status using standard fnd concurrent request screen for= the completion.

<= ![endif]>

Spot check the profi= les you have loaded into the system by browsing the Customer Standard Form. (You ha= ve to check the completion of all the requests under the request set that was submitted in the background. Once al the concurrent requests are completed, then only the changes will be available.
